Those fanatical lubavitch kids dug through a wall between the two buildings.The building next door, which used to be an underground ritual bath, stored the old furniture and stuff (including some old dirty mattresses which were probably wet and dirty from lying on rubble and filth in that abandoned basement). Those kids are religious zealots who strongly believe that their late rebbe is the messiah and they are trying to do what they believe 'he' wanted - to expand the building!   There is nothing to be horrified about here except their total disregard for public safety. Without proper building plans and licenses, parts of the womens' section could have collapsed.   Again, there were rooms already under those two buildings and they only dug out a little bit to make some sort of a 'connection'. Most of the violent 'cult' faction believes the rebbe is 'not' dead and is really in 'hiding'. They are the ones behind all those huge yellow flags and yellow pins on their jackets and shirts.
